INC-SPECT  .Well-defined peak at 62.7 MeV,full width at half      22856  1   36 
             maximum is 2 MeV containing 50% of neutrons, plus    22856  1   37

SAMPLE     .Square metallic uranium 6*6 cm2, 0.178 mm thick.      22856  1   39 
            Purity 99.98%, density 16.295 gram/cm3.               22856  1   40

             (as it is given in thesis)                           22856  1   47 
           (ERR-SYS,7.,8.) uncertainty of the cross section       22856  1   48 
            absolute scale due to:                                22856  1   49 
           (ERR-1) uncertainty in the measured reference (n,p)    22856  1   50 
                  cross sections (5%),                            22856  1   51 
           (ERR-2) uncertainty in the beam monitoring (2%),       22856  1   52 
           (ERR-3,2.,5.) uncertainty in the statistics in the     22856  1   53 
                         H(n,p) recoil proton peak (2-5%),        22856  1   54 
           (ERR-4) uncertainty in solid angle corrections (1%),   22856  1   55 
           (ERR-5) uncertainty in number of target nuclei, etc.   22856  1   56 
           (DATA-ERR,5.5,) The overall relative uncertainties of  22856  1   57 
           the experimental points in the spectra are about 5.5%, 22856  1   58 
           8.5%, 15.% and 25% for respectively p, d, t and alpha  22856  1   59 
           at 62.7 MeV. They are mainly given by the statistics   22856  1   60 
           in the spectra. At lower ejectile energies, the thick  22856  1   61 
           target corrections contribute with supplementary       22856  1   62 
           uncertainties. For all the other incident neutron      22856  1   63 
           energies (continuum), these values are between 2 and 3 22856  1   64 
           times higher as a consequence of the lower incident    22856  1   65 
           neutron flux.  (info from thesis)                      22856  1   66
